To solve door2's 4-digit lock based on the numbers from paper1 (52) and paper2 (14), we can interleave the digits of both numbers:

- Paper1: 5, 2
- Paper2: 1, 4

Interleaving them gives us the sequence 1, 5, 2, 4. Thus, the code is **1524**.

```python
door2.unlock(1524)
```

To solve this puzzle, we need to determine a four-digit code using the numbers obtained from two torn pieces of paper. The first piece has the number **52**, and the second has **14**. Here’s how we can approach it:

### Key Observations:
1. **Ripped Sides Indicate Order**: Since one piece is ripped on the left and the other on the right, it suggests that their numbers should be placed accordingly.
2. **Combining Numbers**: The numbers from each piece (52 and 14) can be combined in different ways to form a four-digit code.

### Logical Steps:
1. **Placement Based on Rip Sides**:
   - The left-ripped piece (**52**) should come first.
   - The right-ripped piece (**14**) should follow.
   
2. **Possible Combinations**:
   - Directly combining the numbers: **5214**
   - Reversing one or both pieces:
     - Reverse of **52** is **25**, combined with **14**: **2514**
     - Reverse of **14** is **41**, combined with **52**: **5241**
     - Reverse both: **2541**

3. **Testing Combinations**:
   - Start by testing the most straightforward combination: **5214**.
   - If that doesn’t work, try reversing one piece at a time.

### Conclusion:
The most logical code to start with is **5214**, based on the rip sides indicating their placement. If that doesn't work, proceed with the reversed combinations.

To solve this puzzle, we need to determine a four-digit code using the numbers obtained from two torn pieces of paper. The first piece has the number **52**, and the second has **14**. Here’s how we can approach it:

### Key Observations:
1. **Ripped Sides Indicate Order**: Since one piece is ripped on the left and the other on the right, it suggests that their numbers should be placed accordingly.
2. **Combining Numbers**: The numbers from each piece (52 and 14) can be combined in different ways to form a four-digit code.

### Logical Steps:
1. **Placement Based on Rip Sides**:
   - The left-ripped piece (**52**) should come first.
   - The right-ripped piece (**14**) should follow.
   
2. **Possible Combinations**:
   - Directly combining the numbers: **5214**
   - Reversing one or both pieces:
     - Reverse of **52** is **25**, combined with **14**: **2514**
     - Reverse of **14** is **41**, combined with **52**: **5241**
     - Reverse both: **2541**

3. **Testing Combinations**:
   - Start by testing the most straightforward combination: **5214**.
   - If that doesn’t work, try reversing one piece at a time.

### Conclusion:
The most logical code to start with is **5214**, based on the rip sides indicating their placement. If that doesn't work, proceed with the reversed combinations.

Step-by-Step Explanation:

1. **Identify Clues**: In room2, there are two papers:
   - Paper1 (torn on the left) with numbers 5 and 2.
   - Paper2 (torn on the right) with numbers 1 and 4.

2. **Interpret Rips as Placement**:
   - The left rip suggests Paper1's number comes from the left side of the code.
   - The right rip suggests Paper2's number is placed on the right side.

3. **Combine Numbers Differently**: Instead of directly concatenating, consider placing Paper2's numbers first (right side) and then Paper1's (left side). This would invert the order.

4. **Form the Code**:
   - Place Paper2's 14 on the left and Paper1's 52 on the right.
   - This gives the code **1452**.
